	<script type="text/javascript" async=true>
	(function() {
		var host = window.location.hostname;
		var element = document.createElement('script');
		var firstScript = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
		var url = 'https://cmp.quantcast.com'
			.concat('/choice/', 'GANCBjEfRH5Fe', '/', host, '/choice.js?tag_version=V2');
		var uspTries = 0;
		var uspTriesLimit = 3;
		element.async = true;
		element.type = 'text/javascript';
		element.src = url;

		firstScript.parentNode.insertBefore(element, firstScript);

		function makeStub() {
			var TCF_LOCATOR_NAME = '__tcfapiLocator';
			var queue = [];
			var win = window;
			var cmpFrame;

			function addFrame() {
				var doc = win.document;
				var otherCMP = !!(win.frames[TCF_LOCATOR_NAME]);

				if (!otherCMP) {
					if (doc.body) {
						var iframe = doc.createElement('iframe');

						iframe.style.cssText = 'display:none';
						iframe.name = TCF_LOCATOR_NAME;
						doc.body.appendChild(iframe);
					} else {
						setTimeout(addFrame, 5);
					}
				}
				return !otherCMP;
			}

			function tcfAPIHandler() {
				var gdprApplies;
				var args = arguments;

				if (!args.length) {
					return queue;
				} else if (args[0] === 'setGdprApplies') {
					if (
						args.length > 3 &&
						args[2] === 2 &&
						typeof args[3] === 'boolean'
					) {
						gdprApplies = args[3];
						if (typeof args[2] === 'function') {
							args[2]('set', true);
						}
					}
				} else if (args[0] === 'ping') {
					var retr = {
						gdprApplies: gdprApplies,
						cmpLoaded: false,
						cmpStatus: 'stub'
					};

					if (typeof args[2] === 'function') {
						args[2](retr);
					}
				} else {
					if(args[0] === 'init' && typeof args[3] === 'object') {
						args[3] = Object.assign(args[3], { tag_version: 'V2' });
					}
					queue.push(args);
				}
			}

			function postMessageEventHandler(event) {
				var msgIsString = typeof event.data === 'string';
				var json = {};

				try {
					if (msgIsString) {
						json = JSON.parse(event.data);
					} else {
						json = event.data;
					}
				} catch (ignore) {}

				var payload = json.__tcfapiCall;

				if (payload) {
					window.__tcfapi(
						payload.command,
						payload.version,
						function(retValue, success) {
							var returnMsg = {
								__tcfapiReturn: {
									returnValue: retValue,
									success: success,
									callId: payload.callId
								}
							};
							if (msgIsString) {
								returnMsg = JSON.stringify(returnMsg);
							}
							if (event && event.source && event.source.postMessage) {
								event.source.postMessage(returnMsg, '*');
							}
						},
						payload.parameter
					);
				}
			}

			while (win) {
				try {
					if (win.frames[TCF_LOCATOR_NAME]) {
						cmpFrame = win;
						break;
					}
				} catch (ignore) {}

				if (win === window.top) {
					break;
				}
				win = win.parent;
			}
			if (!cmpFrame) {
				addFrame();
				win.__tcfapi = tcfAPIHandler;
				win.addEventListener('message', postMessageEventHandler, false);
			}
		};

		makeStub();

		var uspStubFunction = function() {
			var arg = arguments;
			if (typeof window.__uspapi !== uspStubFunction) {
				setTimeout(function() {
					if (typeof window.__uspapi !== 'undefined') {
						window.__uspapi.apply(window.__uspapi, arg);
					}
				}, 500);
			}
		};

		var checkIfUspIsReady = function() {
			uspTries++;
			if (window.__uspapi === uspStubFunction && uspTries < uspTriesLimit) {
				console.warn('USP is not accessible');
			} else {
				clearInterval(uspInterval);
			}
		};

		if (typeof window.__uspapi === 'undefined') {
			window.__uspapi = uspStubFunction;
			var uspInterval = setInterval(checkIfUspIsReady, 6000);
		}
	})();
	</script>

					<h1 class="m-content__title" itemprop="headline">How To Read the Hebrew Alphabet</h1>

											<p class="m-content__subtitle">Known as the Aleph Bet, the Hebrew alphabet contains 22 letters.</p>
					
					<p class="m-content__meta">

					<p>The Hebrew alphabet, or the Aleph Bet, consists of 22 letters. The Aleph Bet is also used to write other Jewish languages, like Yiddish, Ladino, Aramaic, Judeo-Persian and Judeo-Arabic. <p>In Hebrew, the letters are all consonants and the language is comprehensible when written without vowels. However, some texts do include vowels, which are represented in writing by a set of marks, mostly dots and dashes, written under and between the letters. Sacred texts and books for children who are still learning the language are commonly written with vowels. Other texts, like newspapers and books for adults, are written without.</p><p>Unlike English, Hebrew does not have uppercase and lowercase versions of each letter. However, some letters do have a second form that is used in the final position of a word. This is because in ancient times Hebrew was written without spaces between words and these letters helped differentiate where one word ended and another began. </p><p><a href="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/hebrew-word-of-the-day/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"><em><strong>Want to learn Hebrew one day at a time? Click here to sign up for our Hebrew Word of the Day email</strong></em>.</a></p>			<div id="mjl-teads-ad" class="mjl-teads-ad"></div>
			<p>Modern Hebrew has a separate script for handwriting, although scribes use the block script pictured below when handwriting sacred scrolls like a <em><a href="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/what-is-a-mezuzah/">mezuzah</a></em> or a <a href="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/torah-scroll/">Torah</a>.</p><p>Each modern Hebrew letter, as well as its corresponding English sound and its <a href="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/gematria/">numerical value</a>, is listed below. Note that two letters make no sound at all. Scroll all the way down to see the vowels as well.</p><p><strong><a href="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/MJL-Aleph-Bet-Guide-Printable.pdf">Click here for a printable guide to the Aleph Bet.</a></strong></p><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187206" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/1-1/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/1-1.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="1-1" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/1-1.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/1-1.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/1-1.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187206" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/1-1.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/1-1-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/1-1-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Aleph</strong><br>Sound: Silent<br>Numerical value: 1<br>Example: &#1488;&#1460;&#1502;&#1464;&#1488; (<em>ima</em>, meaning &ldquo;mother&rdquo;) </p><div style="height:18px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">

<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187213" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/8-2/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/8.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="8" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/8.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/8.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/8.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187213" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/8.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/8-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/8-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Chet</strong><br>Sound: Gutteral Ch/Kh<br>Numerical value: 8<br>Example: &#1495;&#1463;&#1490; (<em>chag</em>, meaning &ldquo;holiday&rdquo; or &ldquo;festival&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:16px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187214" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/attachment/9/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/9.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="9" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/9.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/9.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/9.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187214" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/9.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/9-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/9-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Tet</strong><br>Sound: T<br>Numerical value: 9<br>Example: &#1496;&#1460;&#1497;&#1505;&#1464;&#1468;&#1492; (<em>tisa</em>, meaning &ldquo;flight&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:16px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">

<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187216" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/attachment/11/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="11" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187216" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Khaf / Kaf</strong><br>Sound: K with the <em>dagesh</em> (dot); gutteral CH/KH without <br>Numerical value: 20<br>Example: &#1499;&#1468;&#1460;&#1497;&#1508;&#1468;&#1464;&#1492; (<em><a href="blank">kippah</a></em>, meaning &ldquo;yarmulke&rdquo; or &ldquo;dome&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:16px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">

<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187218" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/attachment/13/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="13" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187218" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Mem</strong><br>Sound: M<br>Numerical value: 40<br>Example: &#1502;&#1456;&#1504;&#1493;&#1465;&#1512;&#1464;&#1492; (<em><a href="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/the-hanukkiyah-menorah/">menorah</a></em>, meaning &ldquo;lamp&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:16px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187219" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/attachment/14/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="14" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187219" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Nun</strong><br>Sound: N<br>Numerical value: 50<br>Example: &#1504;&#1462;&#1508;&#1462;&#1513;&#1473; (<em>nefesh</em>, meaning &ldquo;soul&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:16px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187220" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/attachment/15/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="15" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187220" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Samech</strong><br>Sound: S<br>Numerical value: 60<br>Example: &#1505;&#1461;&#1508;&#1462;&#1512; (<em>sefer</em>, meaning &ldquo;book&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:16px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187221" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/attachment/16/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/16.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="16" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/16.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/16.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/16.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187221" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/16.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/16-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/16-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Ayin</strong><br>Sound: Silent<br>Numerical value: 70<br>Example: &#1506;&#1460;&#1489;&#1456;&#1512;&#1460;&#1497;&#1514; (<em>ivrit</em>, meaning &ldquo;Hebrew&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:16px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187222" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/attachment/17/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/17.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="17" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/17.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/17.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/17.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187222" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/17.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/17-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/17-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Pey / Fey</strong><br>Sound: P with the&nbsp;<em>dagesh</em>&nbsp;(dot); F without<br>Numerical value: 80<br>Example: &#1508;&#1468;&#1460;&#1500;&#1456;&#1508;&#1468;&#1461;&#1500; (<em>pilpel</em>, meaning &ldquo;pepper&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:16px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187223" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/attachment/18/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/18.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="18" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/18.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/18.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/18.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187223" style="width:150px;height:150px" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/18.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/18-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/18-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Tzadi</strong><br>Sound: Tz or Ts<br>Numerical value: 90<br>Example: &#1510;&#1456;&#1491;&#1464;&#1511;&#1464;&#1492; (<em><a href="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/tzedakah-101/">tzedakah</a></em>, meaning &ldquo;charity&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:16px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187224" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/attachment/19/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/19.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="19" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/19.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/19.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/19.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187224" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/19.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/19-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/19-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Kuf</strong><br>Sound: K<br>Numerical value: 100<br>Example: &#1511;&#1464;&#1492;&#1464;&#1500; (<em>kahal</em>, meaning &ldquo;community&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:16px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187225" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/attachment/20/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/20.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="20" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/20.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/20.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/20.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187225" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/20.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/20-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/20-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Reysh</strong><br>Sound: R<br>Numerical value: 200<br>Example: &#1512;&#1463;&#1489; (<em>rav</em>, meaning &ldquo;rabbi&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:16px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187263" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-8/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-8.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="mjl-aleph-bet-150&#215;150-8" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-8.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-8.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-8.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187263" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-8.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-8-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-8-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Shin / Sin</strong> <br>Sound: Sh when the dot is on the right; S when the dot is on the left<br>Numerical value: 300<br>Example: &#1513;&#1473;&#1463;&#1489;&#1468;&#1464;&#1514; (<em>shabbat</em>, meaning &ldquo;sabbath&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:16px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187227" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/attachment/22/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/22.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="22" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/22.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/22.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/22.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187227" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/22.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/22-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/22-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Taf</strong><br>Sound: T<br>Numerical value: 400<br>Example: &#1514;&#1456;&#1468;&#1508;&#1460;&#1497;&#1500;&#1464;&#1492; (<em><a href="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/category/pray/">tefilah</a></em>, meaning &ldquo;prayer&rdquo;)</p><p></p><div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><h2 class="wp-block-heading">Final Forms (<em>Sofit</em>)</h2><p>Five letters have a distinct final form that is used if the letter ends a word. </p><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187238" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/11-1/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11-1.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="11-1" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11-1.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11-1.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11-1.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187238" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11-1.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11-1-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/11-1-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Mem Sofit</strong><br>Sound: M<br>Example: &#1488;&#1464;&#1491;&#1493;&#1465;&#1501; (<em>adom</em>, meaning &ldquo;red&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187239" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/12-1/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/12-1.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="12-1" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/12-1.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/12-1.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/12-1.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187239" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/12-1.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/12-1-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/12-1-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Nun Sofit</strong><br>Sound: N<br>Example: &#1497;&#1463;&#1497;&#1460;&#1503; (<em>ya-yeen</em>, meaning &ldquo;wine&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187240" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/13-1/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13-1.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="13-1" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13-1.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13-1.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13-1.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187240" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13-1.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13-1-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/13-1-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Tzadi Sofit</strong><br>Sound: Tz or Ts<br>Example: &#1488;&#1462;&#1512;&#1462;&#1509; (<em>eretz</em>, meaning &ldquo;land&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187241" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/14-1/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14-1.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="14-1" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14-1.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14-1.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14-1.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187241" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14-1.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14-1-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/14-1-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Pey / Fey Sofit</strong><br>Sound: F<br>Example: &#1495;&#1465;&#1512;&#1462;&#1507; (<em>choref</em>, meaning &ldquo;winter&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187242" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/15-1/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15-1.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="15-1" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15-1.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15-1.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15-1.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187242" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15-1.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15-1-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/15-1-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Kaf / Khaf Sofit</strong><br>Sound: Guttural Kh<br>Example: &#1502;&#1462;&#1500;&#1462;&#1498; (<em>melekh</em>, meaning &ldquo;king&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><h2 class="wp-block-heading">Vowels (<em>Nikkudot</em>)</h2><p>Each vowel sound in Hebrew corresponds with a nikkud (Hebrew for &ldquo;dot&rdquo;). Many prayer books and dictionaries include nikkudot, while Hebrew-language literature, newspapers, signs and other written materials typically do not. </p><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187230" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="mjl-aleph-bet-150&#215;150-1" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187230" style="width:150px;height:150px" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Kamatz</strong><br>Sound: ah<br>Example: &#1488;&#1464;&#1491;&#1493;&#1465;&#1501; (<em>adom</em>, meaning &ldquo;red&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:6px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187231" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1-1/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1-1.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="mjl-aleph-bet-150&#215;150-1-1" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1-1.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1-1.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1-1.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187231" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1-1.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1-1-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-1-1-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Patach</strong><br>Sound: ah<br>Example: &#1488;&#1463;&#1495;&#1458;&#1512;&#1461;&#1497; (<em>acharei</em>, meaning &ldquo;after&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:6px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187281" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-10/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-10.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="mjl aleph bet 150&#215;150 (10)" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-10.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-10.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-10.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187281" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-10.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-10-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-10-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Sh&rsquo;va</strong><br>Sound: uh or ih<br>Example: &#1489;&#1456;&#1468;&#1497;&#1463;&#1495;&#1463;&#1491; (<em>beyachad</em>, meaning &ldquo;together&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:6px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">

<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187234" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-4/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-4.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="mjl-aleph-bet-150&#215;150-4" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-4.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-4.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-4.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187234" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-4.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-4-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-4-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Segol</strong><br>Sound: eh<br>Example: &#1488;&#1462;&#1513;&#1473;&#1499;&#1468;&#1493;&#1465;&#1500;&#1460;&#1497;&#1493;&#1465;&#1514;&nbsp; (<em>eshkoli&rsquo;ot</em>, meaning &ldquo;grapefruit&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:6px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187235" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-5/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-5.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="mjl-aleph-bet-150&#215;150-5" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-5.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-5.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-5.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187235" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-5.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-5-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-5-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Shuruk</strong><br>Sound: oo<br>Example: &#1510;&#1456;&#1504;&#1460;&#1497;&#1506;&#1493;&#1468;&#1514;&nbsp; (<em>tzniut</em>, meaning &ldquo;modesty&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:6px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187236" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-6/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-6.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="mjl-aleph-bet-150&#215;150-6" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-6.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-6.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-6.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187236" style="width:150px;height:150px" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-6.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-6-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-6-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Cholam</strong><br>Sound: oh<br>Example: &#1506;&#1493;&#1465;&#1500;&#1464;&#1501;&nbsp; (<em>olam</em>, meaning &ldquo;world&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:6px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="alignleft size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" data-attachment-id="187280" data-permalink="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/article/how-to-read-the-hebrew-alphabet/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-9/" data-orig-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-9.png" data-orig-size="150,150" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="mjl-aleph-bet-150&#215;150-9" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-9.png" data-large-file="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-9.png" src="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-9.png" alt="" class="wp-image-187280" srcset="https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-9.png 150w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-9-95x95.png 95w, https://www.myjewishlearning.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/mjl-aleph-bet-150x150-9-88x88.png 88w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" /></figure></div><p><strong>Kubutz</strong><br>Sound: oo<br>Example: &#1513;&#1467;&#1473;&#1500;&#1456;&#1495;&#1464;&#1503;&nbsp;(<em>shulchan</em>, meaning &ldquo;table&rdquo;)</p><div style="height:6px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><p>Nikkudot can also be used with consonants to distinguish between two similar sounds. The dagesh<strong><em> </em></strong>that distinguishes the letters bet/vet, khaf/kaf, and pey/fey is one example. </p><div class="wp-block-group is-layout-flow wp-block-group-is-layout-flow"><div class="wp-block-group__inner-container"></div></div></p>
